9-32 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 12, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/calderaro.jpg)
By Marc Calderaro











  

Though we can all often get preoccupied with the eight top decks, there are always tons more strong decklists just outside the elite eight. Below are the 9th place through 32nd place decklists from Grand Prix Pittsburgh.


  







#### Robert Graves' Four-Color Copycat – GP Pittsburgh, 9th


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
